Fun fact, none of those people actually own any of those apes. NFTs are not the picture. The NFT is essentially a ticket saying "I am allowed to stand next to this work of art." Which in itself is stupid enough regardless of the price tag.  Think of it as a long queue line with a picture at every position in line. The NFTs that you buy are the digital equivalent of one position in the line which is represented with "picture x." You can buy as many spots in line as you want, but none of the posters on the wall belongs to you. Nobody who buys an NFT buys the picture, nor do they buy the rights to the picture. It's a complete scam.

Haha screenshot time. But nah here's some reason NOT to buy an NFT besides it being Just a jpeg  1. For something to have wealth it needs to be wanted or backed by monetary items. the only way you could ever gain back the money spent on an NFT is if someone wanted your specific image. Which they can just as easily screenshot/download. 2. Exclusivity isn't a good marketing standpoint for a number of reasons. For NFT's yes you might own the image outright but unless you copyright it which to my understanding you can't since they are trademarked by boredape or any other NFT company they own almost all rights to said images or there lookalikes it can't be taken down unlike for example music. 3. Most NFT's are get rich quick schemes on the creators part and could cost multiple people thousands for nothing. 4. You gain nothing. I would understand spending millions on a painting since it is genuinely one of a kind or actual stocks but an algorithmic generated image could never compare to artwork. Real artists who put time and effort into their pieces can demand high prices but when the reasoning behind costing so much is due to its "Exclusivity" and zero effort on the creators part you have to step back and think about what your doing. Should I spend money on something I will never see a return from or spend it on lehit anything else.  Maybe you like the idea of owning a several thousand dollar jpeg.  Perhaps you want the bragging rights to say you own a downloadable image worth more than most people's house's.  I'm in no position to say what you do with your money. I could care less if you bought an NFT. I don't want to know. I just want to explain why that's a bad decision and you will never see that money again. But if your rich enough to buy an NFT good for you. us common folk don't have the money to buy a shitty edited pic of a monkey. but the financial crisis is a topic for another day.
